building_colony_shelter = {
	base_buildtime = 180
	planet_unique = yes
	capital = yes
	level = 0
	
	cost = {
	}
	
	produced_resources = {
		energy = 1
	}
	
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_hive
			}
			resources = {
				unity = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			is_ai = yes
			NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			root = {
				food < 1
			}
			resources = {
				food = 25
			}
		}
	}
	
	planet_modifier = {
		pop_government_ethic_attraction = 0.05
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
	
	potential = {
		NOT = {
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = {
				has_building_colony_shelter = yes
				has_building_capital_1 = yes
				has_building_capital_2 = yes
				has_building_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	
	upgrades = {
		building_capital_1
	}
	ai_replace = no
}
building_capital_1_direct_build = {
	base_buildtime = 540
	planet_unique = yes
	capital = yes
	level = 1
	
	cost = {
		minerals = 300
		energy = 300
	}
	
	produced_resources = {
		energy = 4
		unity = 1
	}
	
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_hive
			}
			resources = {
				unity = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			is_ai = yes
			NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			root = {
				food < 1
			}
			resources = {
				food = 25
			}
		}
	}
	
	adjacency_bonus = {
		tile_building_resource_minerals_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_food_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_energy_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_physics_research_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_society_research_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_engineering_research_add = 1
	}
	
	planet_modifier = {
		pop_government_ethic_attraction = 0.1
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
	
	potential = {
		NOT = {
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_colonial_centralization" }
			NOT = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_pops_10"
				planet = {
					count_pops = {
						count > 9
						limit = {
							is_colony_pop = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requires_pops_5"
			planet = {
				count_pops = {
					count > 4
					limit = {
						is_colony_pop = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	upgrades = {
		building_capital_2
	}
	
	prerequisites = {
		"tech_planetary_government"
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		planet = {
			count_pops = {
				count > 5
				limit = {
					is_colony_pop = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_replace = no
	icon = building_capital_1
}

	}

		country_resource_unity_mult = 0.10
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
	
	potential = {
		owner = {
			NOR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
			}
		}
		planet = {
			is_capital = yes
			NOR = {
				has_building_temple = yes
				has_building_holotemple = yes
				has_building_citadel_of_faith = yes
				has_building_sacred_nexus = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	destroy_if = {
		OR = {
			OR = {
				planet = { is_capital = no }
				AND = {
					exists = owner
					owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				AND = {
					has_tradition = tr_supremacy_finish
					has_tradition = tr_harmony_finish
					has_tradition = tr_prosperity_finish
					has_tradition = tr_domination_finish
					has_tradition = tr_expansion_finish
					has_tradition = tr_discovery_finish
					has_tradition = tr_diplomacy_finish
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requires_any_empire_capital"
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_building_capital_3 = yes
					has_building_hab_capital = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	prerequisites = {
		"tech_autocurating_vault"
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		AND = {
			OR = {
				tile = {
					has_building = no
					has_building_autocurating_vault = yes
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				has_resource = {
					type = sr_betharian
					amount > 0
				}
				has_resource = {
					type = sr_alien_pets
					amount > 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = 10000
		modifier = {
			weight = 0
			OR = {
				tile = {
					has_resource = {
						type = energy
						amount > 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			weight = 0
			AND = {
				owner = {
					has_tradition = tr_supremacy_finish
					has_tradition = tr_harmony_finish
					has_tradition = tr_prosperity_finish
					has_tradition = tr_domination_finish
					has_tradition = tr_expansion_finish
					has_tradition = tr_discovery_finish
					has_tradition = tr_diplomacy_finish
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_replace = no

			}

				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}

				has_building_slave_processing = yes

					limit = { is_enslaved = yes }
					count > 2
				}
			}
		}
	}

			weight = 1000000

						type = minerals
						amount > 0
					}
				}
			}

			weight = 10
			factor = 2

				tile = {

						type = food
						amount > 0
					}
					has_resource = {
						type = minerals
						amount > 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			weight = 1
			factor = 1
			and = {
				tile = {

						type = energy
						amount = 0

building_basic_farm = {
	tags = { hydroponics_farm }
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_0
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @resource_building_mineral_cost_tier_0
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
	
	potential = {
		NOT = {
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			OR = {
				has_building_colony_shelter = yes
				has_building_deployment_post = yes
			}
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_eco_simulation" }
			NOT = {
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "requires_building_capital_1"
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_building_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		OR = {
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			AND = {
				owner = {
					has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_harmony_utopian_dream
				}
				NOT = {
					planet = {
						has_building_paradise_dome = yes
					}
				}
				OR = {
					planet = {
						has_building_hydroponics_farm_2 = yes
					}
					planet = {
						has_building_hydroponics_farm_3 = yes
					}

						has_building_hydroponics_farm_4 = yes
					}
					planet = {
						has_building_hydroponics_farm_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	produced_resources = {
		food = @resource_building_output_tier_0
	}
	
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
			NOT = { has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish }
			resources = {
				unity = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll }
			resources = {
				minerals = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
			resources = {
				unity = 1
				minerals = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			is_ai = yes
			NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			root = {
				food < 2
			}
			resources = {
				food = 5
			}
		}
	}
	
	required_resources = {
		energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_0
	}
	
	upgrades = {
		building_hydroponics_farm_1
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		OR = {
			tile = {
				has_building = no
			}
			tile = {
				has_building_basic_farm = yes
			}
		}
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}

			weight = 10

				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}

			}

					OR = {
						has_building_capital_1 = yes
						has_building_capital_2 = yes
						has_building_capital_3 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		exists = owner

			AND = {
				owner = {
					has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_harmony_utopian_dream
				}
				owner = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				NOT = {

						has_building_paradise_dome = yes
					}
				}

					planet = {

					}
					planet = {
						has_building_hydroponics_farm_3 = yes
					}
					planet = {
						has_building_hydroponics_farm_4 = yes
					}
					planet = {
						has_building_hydroponics_farm_5 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requires_building_capital_1"
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_building_capital_1 = yes
					has_building_capital_2 = yes
					has_building_capital_3 = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		OR = {
			tile = {
				has_building = no
			}
			tile = {
				has_building_basic_farm = yes
			}
			tile = {

				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0

				}

building_basic_mine = {
	tags = { mining_network }
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_0
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			OR = {
				has_building_colony_shelter = yes
				has_building_deployment_post = yes
			}
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_basic_industry" }
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_capital_1"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building_capital_1 = yes
							has_building_capital_2 = yes
							has_building_capital_3 = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = "requires_building_machine_capital_1"
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes

	}

					has_building_capital_3 = yes
				}
			}
		}

	}

				has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
			}
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			NOR = {
				has_building_autochthon_monument = yes
				has_building_heritage_site = yes
				has_building_hypercomms_forum = yes
				has_building_autocurating_vault = yes
			}
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_holographic_rituals" }
			owner = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
			}
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
				NOR = {
					has_building_autochthon_monument = yes
					has_building_heritage_site = yes
					has_building_hypercomms_forum = yes

						has_building_capital_1 = yes

						has_building_capital_3 = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }

				owner = {
					has_tradition = tr_supremacy_finish
					has_tradition = tr_harmony_finish
					has_tradition = tr_prosperity_finish
					has_tradition = tr_domination_finish
					has_tradition = tr_expansion_finish
					has_tradition = tr_discovery_finish
					has_tradition = tr_diplomacy_finish
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	upgrades = {
		building_holotemple
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		OR = {
			tile = {
				has_building = no
			}
			tile = {
				has_building_temple = yes
			}
		}
		NOR = {
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_betharian
				amount > 0
			}
			has_resource = {
				type = sr_alien_pets
				amount > 0
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = 10000
		modifier = {
			weight = 0
			OR = {
				tile = {
					has_resource = {
						type = energy
						amount > 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			weight = 0
			AND = {
				owner = {
					has_tradition = tr_supremacy_finish
					has_tradition = tr_harmony_finish
					has_tradition = tr_prosperity_finish
					has_tradition = tr_domination_finish
					has_tradition = tr_expansion_finish
					has_tradition = tr_discovery_finish
					has_tradition = tr_diplomacy_finish
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_replace = no

				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requires_building_capital_2"
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
					has_building_machine_capital_3 = yes
					has_building_hab_capital = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	prerequisites = {
		"tech_hypercomms_forum"
	}
	
	upgrades = {
		building_alpha_hub
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		# If planet only has slaves/robots, keep it to mining and farming...
		is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = 10000
	}
	ai_replace = no
	icon = building_system_conflux
}
building_system_conflux = {
	base_buildtime = @planet_unique_build_time_3
	is_listed = no
	planet_unique = yes
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @planet_unique_mineral_cost_3
		energy = @planet_unique_energy_cost_3
	}
	
	produced_resources = {
		unity = 6
	}
	
	required_resources = {
		energy = @planet_unique_upkeep_3
	}
	
	planet_modifier = {
		tile_resource_unity_mult = 0.10
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	
	potential = {
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	
	destroy_if = {
		OR = {
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			owner = {
				AND = {
					has_tradition = tr_supremacy_finish
					has_tradition = tr_harmony_finish
					has_tradition = tr_prosperity_finish
					has_tradition = tr_domination_finish
					has_tradition = tr_expansion_finish
					has_tradition = tr_discovery_finish
					has_tradition = tr_diplomacy_finish
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = "requires_building_capital_2"
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
					has_building_machine_capital_3 = yes
					has_building_hab_capital = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	prerequisites = {
		"tech_hypercomms_forum"
	}
	
	upgrades = {
		building_alpha_hub
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		# If planet only has slaves/robots, keep it to mining and farming...
		is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = 10000
	}
	ai_replace = no
}
